<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:нотный.html>но́тный</a> (21228)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нота.html>но́ты</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nóty</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***ночевать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ночевать.html>ночева́ть</a> (3187)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ночь.html>ночь</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nočʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ева́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-evátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ночевать.html>ночева́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nočevátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заночевать.html>заночева́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:переночевать.html>переночева́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to stay for the night, to stay overnight
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:где.html>Где</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ты.html>ты</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ночевать.html>ночева́л</a></b>? - <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>Я</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ночевать.html>ночева́л</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:друг.html>дру́га</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Gde ty <b>nočevál</b>? - Ja <b>nočevál</b> u drúga.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Where did you spend last night? - I stayed overnight at a friend's place.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***ночка.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ночка.html>но́чка</a> (17681)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ночь.html>ночь</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nočʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ночлег.html>ночле́г</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nočlég</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ночлег.html>ночле́га</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ночлег.html>ночле́ги</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ночлег.html>ночле́гов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>lodging for the night
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:искать.html>иска́ть</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ночлег.html>ночле́га</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">iskátʹ <b>nočléga</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">seek lodging/shelter for the night</span></div></dd>

<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:остаться.html>оста́ться</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:без.html>без</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ночлег.html>ночле́га</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ostátʹsja bez <b>nočléga</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">find oneself no shelter for the night</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>overnight stay
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:остановиться.html>останови́ться</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ночлег.html>ночле́г</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ostanovítʹsja na <b>nočlég</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">stay overnight</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ночь.html>ночь</a> (169)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv"><a href = vnd.unilang:ночь.html>ночь</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nočĭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*noťь</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*nókʷts</i>. Doublet of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">нощь</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">noščʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">night (archaic)</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, borrowed from Old Church Slavonic.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ношение.html>ноше́ние</a> (20233)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:носить.html>носи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nosítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-е́ние</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-énije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ношение.html>ноше́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nošénije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ношение.html>ноше́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ношение.html>ноше́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ношение.html>ноше́ний</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>carrying</li>
<li>wearing (clothes)</li>
<li>bearing (a child)</li></ol>

***ноябрь.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ноябрь.html>ноя́брь</a> (2230)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">ноѩбрь</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nojębrĭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Medieval_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Medieval Greek">Byzantine Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">Νοέμβριος</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">Noémbrios</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">november</i>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">novem</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*h₁néwn̥</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">nine</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">-ber</i> from <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">-bris</i>, an adjectival suffix.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ноябрь.html>ноя́брь</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nojábrʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ноябрь.html>ноября́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ноябрь.html>ноябри́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ноябрь.html>ноябре́й</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>November
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ноябрь.html>ноябре́</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">v <b>nojabré</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">in November</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ноябрь.html>ноябре́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́того</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:год.html>го́да</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">v <b>nojabré</b> étovo góda</i> ― <span class="e-translation">in November</span></div></dd>

<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">нравъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nravŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*norvъ</i>. Doublet of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:норов.html>но́ров</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nórov</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, the inherited East Slavic form.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нрав.html>нрав</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nrav</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нрав.html>нра́ва</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нрав.html>нра́вы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нрав.html>нра́вов</a></b>)

***нравиться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:нравиться.html>нра́виться</a> (627)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нрав.html>нрав</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nrav</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ить</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-itʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нравиться.html>нра́виться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nrávitʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:понравиться.html>понра́виться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to like (<i>the person who likes takes the dative case</i>)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>мне</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:нравиться.html>нра́вится</a></b>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">On mne <b>nrávitsja</b>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I <b>like</b> him.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>Я</a> им <b><a href = vnd.unilang:нравиться.html>нра́влюсь</a></b>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ja im <b>nrávljusʹ</b>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">They <b>like</b> me.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>Мне</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:нравиться.html>нра́вятся</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:блюдо.html>блю́да</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:из.html>из</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:курица.html>ку́рицы</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Mne <b>nrávjatsja</b> bljúda iz kúricy.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I <b>love</b> chicken dishes.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to please</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нрав.html>нрав</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nrav</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-o-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:учение.html>уче́ние</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">učénije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нравоучение.html>нравоуче́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nravoučénije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нравоучение.html>нравоуче́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нравоучение.html>нравоуче́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нравоучение.html>нравоуче́ний</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>moral instruction, moral edification, moralizing</li>
<li>moral <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">at the end of a story</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:нравственный.html>нра́вственный</a> (4113)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">нра́вство</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nrávstvo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-енный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ennyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нравственный.html>нра́вственный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nrávstvennyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)нра́вственнее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)нра́вственней</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>moral <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">referring to morality</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:нравственный.html>нра́вственные</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:правило.html>пра́вила</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nrávstvennyje</b> právila</i> ― <span class="e-translation">moral rules, rules of morality</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>moral, ethical <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">conforming to a standard of right behavior</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:очень.html>о́чень</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:нравственный.html>нра́вственный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:человек.html>челове́к</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">óčenʹ <b>nrávstvennyj</b> čelovék</i> ― <span class="e-translation">very moral person</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***ну.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ну.html>ну</a> (71)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*nъ</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Balto-Slavic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Balto-Slavic language">Proto-Balto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-bsl-pro">*nu</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*nu</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Interjection">Interjection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ну.html>ну</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nu</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>well
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ну.html>Ну</a></b>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Nu</b>!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Well! (indicating surprise and a little disbelief)</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ну.html>Ну</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ж.html>ж</a>?</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Nu</b> što ž?</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Well, what?</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ну.html>Ну</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:так.html>так</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:же.html>же</a>?</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Nu</b> tak štó že?</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Well, what about it?</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:да.html>Да</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ну.html>ну́</a></b>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Da <b>nú</b>!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">No, I don't want to! ("<a href = vnd.unilang:совсем.html>совсе́м</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:хотеть.html>хочу́</a>!" is synonymous)</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:да.html>Да</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ну.html>ну</a></b>?!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Da <b>nu</b>?!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Really?!</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ну.html>ну</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nu</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> yeah, yep (impolite, sometimes implying a question - so what?)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ты.html>Ты</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:читать.html>чита́л</a>? — <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ну.html>Ну</a></b>?</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ty éto čitál? — <b>Nu</b>?</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Have you read this? - Yeah, so what?</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span id=".D0.97.D0.BD.D0.B0.D1.87.D0.B5.D0.BD.D0.B8.D0.B5"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Значение"><a href = vnd.unilang:значение.html>Значе́ние</a></span></h4>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:выражать.html>выража́ет</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:призыв.html>призы́в</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:понукание.html>понука́ние</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:нетерпение.html>нетерпе́ние</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:удивление.html>удивле́ние</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:досада.html>доса́ду</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:или.html>или</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ирония.html>иро́нию</a> <span class="example-fullblock"><ul>
<li><span class="example-block" style="color:black">— <span class="example-select" style="background-color: EDF0FF; font-weight: bold;"><a href = vnd.unilang:ну.html>Ну</a></span>, <a href = vnd.unilang:ехать.html>поезжа́й</a> скорее! </span> <span class="example-fullblock"></li>
<li><span class="example-block" style="color:black"><span class="example-select" style="background-color: EDF0FF; font-weight: bold;"><a href = vnd.unilang:ну.html>Ну</a></span>, <a href = vnd.unilang:опять.html>опя́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мы.html>мы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:опоздать.html>опозда́ли</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:открытие.html>откры́тию</a>! </span></li>
</ul></li>


<li><a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>то</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:же.html>же</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:но.html>но</a> |  <a href = vnd.unilang:возглас.html>во́зглас</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:который.html>кото́рым</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:возница.html>возни́ца</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:понукать.html>понука́ет</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:лошадь.html>ло́шадь</a> <span class="example-fullblock"><ul>
<li><span class="example-block" style="color:black"><span class="example-select" style="background-color: EDF0FF; font-weight: bold;"><a href = vnd.unilang:ну.html>Ну</a></span>, <a href = vnd.unilang:мертвый.html>мёртвая</a>! — <a href = vnd.unilang:крикнуть.html>кри́кнул</a> малюточка <a href = vnd.unilang:бас.html>ба́сом</a>//<a href = vnd.unilang:рвануть.html>Рвану́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:под.html>под</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:уздцы.html>уздцы́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> быстрей <a href = vnd.unilang:зашагать.html>зашага́л</a>. </span></li>

<h4><span id=".D0.A1.D0.B8.D0.BD.D0.BE.D0.BD.D0.B8.D0.BC.D1.8B"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Синонимы"><a href = vnd.unilang:синоним.html>Сино́нимы</a></span></h4>

***нудить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:нудить.html>нуди́ть</a> (29019)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Inherited from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">нꙋдити</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nuditi</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*nuditi</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ukrainian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Ukrainian language">Ukrainian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="uk">нуди́ти</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="uk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nudýty</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Belarusian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Belarusian language">Belarusian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="be">нудзі́ць</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="be-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nudzícʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">ноудити</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nuditi</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to force, to compel</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">нѫдити</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nǫditi</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (per Vasmer, with secondary nasalization), <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bulgarian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Bulgarian language">Bulgarian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="bg"><a href = vnd.unilang:нудить.html>ну́дя</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="bg-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">núdja</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to force, to compel</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Serbo-Croatian" class="extiw" title="w:Serbo-Croatian">Serbo-Croatian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="sh">ну̏дити</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to offer, to obtain</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (1sg. <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="sh">ну̏дӣм</i>), <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Slovene_language" class="extiw" title="w:Slovene language">Slovene</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sl">núditi</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to force</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (1sg. <i class="Latn mention" lang="sl">nȗdim</i>), <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Czech_language" class="extiw" title="w:Czech language">Czech</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="cs">nuditi</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to bore</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Slovak_language" class="extiw" title="w:Slovak language">Slovak</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sk">nudiť</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to bore</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">nudzić</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to bore, to annoy</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нудить.html>ну́дить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">núditʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:принудить.html>прину́дить</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated or low  colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to force, to compel</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated or low  colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to tire, to exhaust</li></ol>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Apparently related to <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нудить.html>ну́дить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">núditʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to compel</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нудить.html>нуди́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nudítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to talk annoyingly or monotonously</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to annoy, to bother</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to cause melancholy, to bore</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to persistently beg, to pester <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">u</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:нудный.html>ну́дно</a> (21111)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нудный.html>ну́дно</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">núdno</span>)
</p>

***нужда.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:нужда.html>нужда́</a> (2971)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">ноужда</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nužda</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*nuďa</i>. Displaced the inherited East Slavic form <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">нужа</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nuža</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Czech_language" class="extiw" title="w:Czech language">Czech</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="cs">nouze</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Slovak_language" class="extiw" title="w:Slovak language">Slovak</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sk">núdza</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Slovene_language" class="extiw" title="w:Slovene language">Slovene</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sl">nuja</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">нужа</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nuža</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нужда.html>нужда́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nuždá</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нужда.html>нужды́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нужда.html>ну́жды</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нужда.html>ну́жд</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>need, want, request</li>
<li>need, indigence</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:потребность.html>потре́бность</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">potrébnostʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:необходимость.html>необходи́мость</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">neobxodímostʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бедность.html>бе́дность</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">bédnostʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нищета.html>нищета́</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">niščetá</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

<ol><li>to need
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Он</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:нуждаться.html>нужда́ется</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:посторонний.html>посторо́нней</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:помощь.html>по́мощи</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">On <b>nuždájetsja</b> v postorónnej pómošči.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">He needs (external) help.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to be hard up, to be needy</li></ol>

***нуждающийся.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:нуждаться.html>нужда́ющийся</a> (16694)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***нужный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:нужный.html>ну́жный</a> (136)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">ну́жа</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">núža</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нужный.html>ну́жный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">núžnyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)нужне́е</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)нужне́й</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>necessary, needed
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>мне</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:нужный.html>ну́жен</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:словарь.html>слова́рь</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">mne <b>núžen</b> slovárʹ.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I need a dictionary.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>мне</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:нужный.html>нужна́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ваш.html>ва́ша</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:помощь.html>по́мощь</a>.</i> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">formal</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">mne <b>nužná</b> váša pómoščʹ.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I need your help.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>Used with the dative or <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:для.html>для</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dlja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + genitive, when speaking of a person (<i>necessary for someone</i>):
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мы.html>нам</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:для.html>для</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мы.html>нас</a>) <b><a href = vnd.unilang:нужный.html>ну́жные</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:деньги.html>де́ньги</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">nam (dlja nas) <b>núžnyje</b> dénʹgi.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">We need money.</span></dd><dd>(literally, “<span class="e-literally">Money is necessary for us.</span>”)</dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>Used with <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:для.html>для</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dlja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + genitive or <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">na</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + accusative, when speaking of an action (<i>necessary to do something</i>):
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:нужный.html>ну́жные</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:для.html>для</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:покупка.html>поку́пки</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:покупка.html>поку́пку</a>) <a href = vnd.unilang:машина.html>маши́ны</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:деньги.html>де́ньги</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>núžnyje</b> dlja pokúpki (na pokúpku) mašíny dénʹgi.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Money is needed to buy a car.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:необходимый.html>необходи́мый</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">neobxodímyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

***нумерация.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:нумерация.html>нумера́ция</a> (31441)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">нумерова́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">numerovátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ция</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ácija</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нумерация.html>нумера́ция</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">numerácija</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нумерация.html>нумера́ции</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нумерация.html>нумера́ции</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нумерация.html>нумера́ций</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>numbering, enumeration</li>
<li>number system</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:нутро.html>нутро́</a> (8608)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*ǫtro</i>.

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li>the inside, the inward nature (especially of a person), gut feeling
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>Я</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:нутро.html>нутро́м</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:чуять.html>чу́ю</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:добро.html>добру́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>всё</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ja <b>nutróm</b> čúju, ne k dobrú vsjó éto.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">I have a <b>gut feeling</b>, this won't mean anything good.</span></dd><dd>(literally, “<span class="e-literally">I feel <b>with</b> [my] <b>inside</b>, not for the good is all this.</span>”)</dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>inside</li></ol>

***ныне.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ныне.html>ны́не</a> (2505)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">нꙑнѣ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nyně</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, compare with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ukrainian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Ukrainian language">Ukrainian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="uk">ни́нi</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="uk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nýni</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li>now, nowadays, today, at present</li></ol>
